<Name>Jorge haro<//Name><Date>1462298004663< /Date><Rate>1< /Rate>< Text>
BUYERS BEWARE!
On Saturday 4/30/16, I purchased an installation kit to install my daughter's stereo, on Sunday I found out that she had already had it installed, on Monday I took back the unopened, unused installation kit, along with my receipt. The individual behind the counter was courteous, but told me that they do not issue refunds, only store credit. I told him that I was not aware of this policy and that it not posted anywhere in the store, he told me it's on the receipt and that it doesn't have to be posted. I insisted that they have to make the consumer aware of this policy prior to purchase and not after they've already taken your cash, in the form of a receipt. When I said this a man sitting next to him, rudely stated that if I didn't like this, to take them to court. I left the store with the item, and looked up California refund law, and sure enough, they are in violation. California  law states that they can issue credit, but that the policy has to be posted in the store, where customers can easily see it, or even on the merchandise itself, and it even specifies that printing it on the receipt does not cover this requirement. Since it is not posted, California law states that I have 7 days to get a cash refund.  The kit was $25, which may not be a lot of money, but at this point, I am strongly leaning towards small claims court, not only because of the principal of the matter, but also because I'm sure they've ripped off, & will continue to rip off other customers that are unaware of their ILLEGAL policy.</Text>

<review>This park is really a small patch of grass in the middle of suburbia, yet it offers an unrxpected charm.  It typically just serves as a rest stop for me while I'm following the bike route on Chatsworth.  I've been pulling my 2 year old and our micro dog along in bike trailer and this gives the two of them a chance to get out and walk together.  The hedges on one side give a bit of privacy that makes you feel your presence isn't too intrusive to the neighborhood.  The park has a slope from the surrounding streets to the middle. <name>John Economides<//name><Date>1478094178721</Date><Rate>2<//Rate><Review>From the outside, this hotel appears to be "quaint". But once you actually get inside your room, you find that it's no different from your run of the mill 20 year old Holiday Inn.
Discolored paint, peeling wall paper, a bathroom that has clearly had a thorough using. Air conditioning unit that still has unit mounted controls. Light bulbs that long ago ceased to be color matched (daylight or soft white people, it's not hard).

There are a few stars here, the bedside alarm clock is completely dimmable to the no light position while retaining alarm functionality. That same clock also has two edison outlets and two USB outlets for charging gadgets. Enough that I didn't have to worry about unpacking my travel power strip.

There's a dorm room sized refrigerator in the room. And a Safeway a mere 8 miles away. There's a microwave in the lobby... but that brings me to my next detraction.

The lobby is only staffed/open from 7AM-10PM. They start serving breakfast at 7AM, so I am curious why the lobby isn't open an hour prior to that. Much less staffed and open 24HR regardless.

I'm only a day in, so I'm sure there will be more things I notice in the coming week. If you're listening, Choice Hotels... you should consider changing your brand standards.< /Review><pics>None</pics><Resp>None< /Resp>< gmapID>

<date>1522710101952</date><Rate>5< /Rate><text>I started training on the Legacy Martial Arts Family Fitness Center program over a year ago. I moved to California and it took me around 4-5 months to find a place that I truly love. I have been studying and training martial arts for over 10 years and I must say that this is one of the best programs in the county.

Some of the things I look for in a good martial arts program is commitment, integrity, family oriented, high intensity training, respect and can also have instructors that are willing to help teach and have the patience to instruct not only adults but children. The family environment in the studio you can feel it from the moment you walk in the studio, they take you in as family.

The instructors at Legacy Martial Arts are all well rounded martial artists. They work with your fundamentals so you can have a great base to keep learning more complicated things. They take your needs and goals to make you the best version of yourself you can be. The instructors are State Champions, District Champions and World Champions ranging from Forms to Sparring. They take your needs whether it is becoming healthier, competitive taekwondo, learning self-defense or just wanting to do something different and learn. Once they know what you are looking for they focus on making you the type of person in the martial arts world you want to become. With your hard work, will come great results, they will push to get the best out of you. They are professionals in what they do and it shows in every action and class they perform. They are known in the county and around the entire USA for their completeness, way of teaching and structured program with in the studio.

Seeing the Tiny Tigers program (children) you can see how creativity meets morals. By mixing fun active learning and respect they teach the children about self-control, integrity, honor, commitment and leadership. The instructors also don‚Äôt stop in teaching your kids about martial arts but how to be a successful leader. They help your child gain more confidence and in a short amount of time that develops into creating leaders, on and off the studio. By implementing creative thinking the instructors also have a system in place to make sure that your child will also try and get better grades in school, be more respectful to other people and have self-control in their actions.

The adult program always has more than twenty adults. Normally the adult classes in other studios I have been in are very low. Some student‚Äôs parents start out bringing their kids and quickly want to join the training themselves. This is the type of family environment that all the instructors bring to this studio. The adults all encourage each other to strive for a better future on and off the studio. One day your training together and the other you are in a gathering having fun and talking about goals, the future and even your professional careers.

As a martial arts competitor for Legacy Martial Arts studio I have learned that if you have a goal and you are willing to put in the work the instructors will take you to that level. They will push you in ways you never thought you could reach, finding out that the barriers you use to put yourself, get taken down with dedication and commitment. The instructors will push you so that you can accomplish your goals and aspirations in your martial arts carrier.

The facilities are top notch. It is a big space that has everything you need. The instructors keep it tidy and clean all the time. There is a spectator section at the entrance of the studio were parents or people can come look at the class before joining. The equipment used in training is also always clean and up to date.

I would refer this place to anyone that is curious about martial arts or wants to keep going on their journey to becoming a better martial artist and person. Between the environment the studio provides and the type of training they provide there is no doubt in my mind if you try it you will understand what I am saying. 1457936553025</Date>
<rate>5< /rate>< text>
There are many great Karate schools in Oxnard, Ventura and Camarillo, but Legacy Martial Arts in Oxnard was the one that impressed. I wanted to find a program that could provide my 3 year old son an opportunity to exercise, have fun, and not to mention continue to learn about self control and focus. Unfortunately for us at the time, many karate schools did not accept students that young. I was willing to wait 6 months until he turned 4 and so my plan was to simply get a head start in my search for the best karate school for my son. I found Legacy Martial Arts online and found out they offer several programs appropriate for any age starting at age 3. My son and I visited the school, he took his first complimentary class and the rest is history. What I have come to admire and love about Tiny Tigers (3-6 years old) program was:

1. Verbal instructions as well as demonstration of movements by instructor are always clear, brief and appropriate for children 3-6 years old.
2. Parent participation. I wasn't expecting to participate at all but it is fun and a great way to learn how to help our children when they practice at home. No need to know karate, kids stand in several lines and we (adults) hold targets or pool noodles to provide students the opportunity to practice in class as much as possible (about 5-8 minutes). This also provides instructors time to go around to help and correct children.
3. Ms. Rosales, the Tiny Tigers instructor, reviews numbers, name of animals, body parts, explains key terms and vocabulary, asks for clarification, reviews sequences and patterns, and uses choral response during class.
4. No memorization is needed, students build and put forms together by working on individual steps and movements.
5. Finally, I especially love and appreciate the collaborative support of other instructors and of that of older karate students during Tiny Tigers class. Tiny Tigers always have the instructor and at least one more person helping in every class.

If I am impressed by this class alone, I can only imagine the quality of instruction and support other students get in their respective program and level!

It has been 5 months and my husband and I as well as the rest of the family, have seen an overall improvement in my son. I have come to like this school so much that as of last week I became a member of their Hyper Fight Club. I love the energy and camaraderie as well as the work out and the support I get from all of the instructors. I'm looking forward to reaching my health and fitness goals.

I want to thank Mr. Gregory, Ms. Rosales, Mr. Medina, as well as the rest of the staff and the many families that make Legacy Martial Arts a GREAT and AMAZING martial arts school.</text>

<Date>1525742296771< /Date><user>101466442122096967700< /user><text>What impressive about this particular Vons is that their fresh produce section is at the front of the store. Most and any other store would have them at the far side or even at the back of the store. So, when I come it, it just feels nice, healthy and open - it doesnt feel crowded at all.
I have been coming in to this store for about a 3 years now, and a lot has changed.
I love that they accept google and apple pay. You can also use those means to pay for your orders at their in-house Jamba Juice and Starbucks. PROTIP: you can pay for your groceries from these outlets, too.
The only one disappointing thing they did which i had wished they kept were the self check out counters; because most of the time, i just go in for 1 or 2 things, and i didnt have to wait in like to pay. These supposed express checkout lanes that replaced the self checkout counters are empty most of the time, and it appears that its just a place to keep returned items to be placed at the end of the day. So, what should just be a quick pick up, becomes several minutes waiting in line at a counter for someone to finish counting change to pay in exact amount.

Other than that, the manager is very friendly when i had inquired about a favorite drink they havent restocked - they restocked it!! - and it sells out fast. - they however havent been restocking or having the party tray mini rolls or the croissants anymore, which is my most frequent buy from there a couple years back, but still - their fresh items are great, and its conveniently surrounded by other shops where you can eat, drink or shop at while a friend or family member is restocking your home's supplies.<//text><rating>4<//rating>< Pictures>
